This also means that the work\\n188:      * will not be parallelized for multiple topics, and the number of tasks will scale with the maximum partition\\n189:      * count of any matching topic rather than the total number of partitions across all topics.\\n190:      * <p>\\n191:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\\n192:      * If this is not the case it is the user's responsibility to repartition the data before any key based operation\\n193:      * (like aggregation or join) is applied to the returned {@link KStream}.\\n194:      *\\n195:      * @param topicPattern the pattern to match for topic names\\n196:      * @return a {@link KStream} for topics matching the regex pattern.\\n197:      */\\n198:     public synchronized <K, V> KStream<K, V> stream(final Pattern topicPattern) {\\n199:         return stream(topicPattern, Consumed.with(null, null));\\n200:     }\\n201: \\n202:     /**\\n203:      * Create a {@link KStream} from the specified topic pattern.\\n204:      * The {@code \\\"auto.offset.reset\\\"} strategy, {@link TimestampExtractor}, key and value deserializers\\n205:      * are defined by the options in {@link Consumed} are used.\\n206:      * <p>\\n207:      * If multiple topics are matched by the specified pattern, the created {@link KStream} will read data from all of\\n208:      * them and there is no ordering guarantee between records from different topics. This also means that the work\\n209:      * will not be parallelized for multiple topics, and the number of tasks will scale with the maximum partition\\n210:      * count of any matching topic rather topics matching the regex pattern.\\n219:      */\\n220:     public synchronized <K, V> KStream<K, V> stream(final Pattern topicPattern,\\n221: null\\\");\\n224:         return internalStreamsBuilder.stream(topicPattern, new ConsumedInternal<>(consumed));\\n225:     }\\n226: \\n227:     /**\\n228:      * Create a {@link KTable} for the specified topic.\\n229:      * The {@code \\\"auto.offset.reset\\\"} strategy, {@link TimestampExtractor}, key and value deserializers\\n230:      * are defined by the options in {@link Consumed} are used.\\n231:      * Input {@link KeyValue records} with {@code null} key will be dropped.\\n232:      * <p>\\n233:      * Note that the specified input topic must be partitioned by key.\\n234:      * If this is not the case the returned {@link KTable} will be corrupted.\\n235:      * <p>\\n236:      * The resulting {@link KTable} will be materialized in a local {@link KeyValueStore} using the given\\n237:      * {@code Materialized} instance.\\n238:      * An internal changelog topic is created by default. Because the source topic can\\n239:      * be used for recovery, you can avoid creating the changelog topic by setting\\n240:      * the {@code \\\"topology.optimization\\\"} to {@code \\\"all\\\"} in the {@link StreamsConfig}.\\n241:      * <p>\\n242:      * You should only specify serdes in the {@link Consumed} instance as these will also be used to overwrite the\\n243:      * serdes in {@link Materialized}, i.e.,\\n244:      * <pre> {@code\\n245:      * streamBuilder.table(topic, Consumed.with(Serde.String(), Serde.String()), Materialized.<String, String, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>as(storeName))\\n246:      * }\\n247:      * </pre>\\n248:      * To query the local {@link ReadOnlyKeyValueStore} it must be obtained via\\n249:      * {@link KafkaStreams#store(StoreQueryParameters) KafkaStreams#store(...)}:\\n250:      * <pre>{@code\\n251:      * KafkaStreams streams = ...\\n252:      * StoreQueryParameters<ReadOnlyKeyValueStore<K, ValueAndTimestamp<V>>> storeQueryParams = StoreQueryParameters.fromNameAndType(queryableStoreName, QueryableStoreTypes.timestampedKeyValueStore());\\n253:      * ReadOnlyKeyValueStore<K, ValueAndTimestamp<V>> localStore = streams.store(storeQueryParams);\\n254:      * K key = \\\"some-key\\\";\\n255:      * ValueAndTimestamp<V> valueForKey = localStore.get(key); // key must be local (application state is shared over all running Kafka Streams instances)\\n256:      * }</pre>\\n257:      * For non-local keys, a custom RPC mechanism must be implemented using {@link KafkaStreams#metadataForAllStreamsClients()} to\\n258:      * query the value of the key on a parallel running instance of your Kafka Streams application.\\n259:      *\\n260:      * @param topic              the topic name; cannot be {@code null}\\n261:      * @param consumed           the instance of {@link Consumed} used to define optional parameters; cannot be {@code null}\\n262:      * @param materialized       the instance of {@link Materialized} used to materialize a state store; cannot be {@code null}\\n263:      * @return a {@link KTable} for the specified topic\\n264:      */\\n265:     public synchronized <K, V> KTable<K, V> table(final String topic,\\n266:                                                   final Consumed<K, V> consumed,\\n267:                                                   final Materialized<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materialized) {\\n268:         Objects.requireNonNull(topic, \\\"topic can't be null\\\");\\n269:         Objects.requireNonNull(consumed, \\\"consumed can't be null\\\");\\n270:         Objects.requireNonNull(materialized, \\\"materialized can't be null\\\");\\n271:         final ConsumedInternal<K, V> consumedInternal = new ConsumedInternal<>(consumed);\\n272:         materialized.withKeySerde(consumedInternal.keySerde()).withValueSerde(consumedInternal.valueSerde());\\n273: \\n274:         final MaterializedInternal<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materializedInternal =\\n275:             new MaterializedInternal<>(materialized, internalStreamsBuilder, topic + \\\"-\\\");\\n276: \\n277:         return internalStreamsBuilder.table(topic, consumedInternal, materializedInternal);\\n278:     }\\n279: \\n280:     /**\\n281:      * Create a {@link KTable} for the specified topic.\\n282:      * The default {@code \\\"auto.offset.reset\\\"} strategy and default key and value deserializers as specified in the\\n283:      * {@link StreamsConfig config} are used.\\n284:      * Input {@link KeyValue records} with {@code null} key will be dropped.\\n285:      * <p>\\n286:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\\n287:      * If this is not the case the returned {@link KTable} will be corrupted.\\n288:      * <p>\\n289:      * The resulting {@link KTable} will be materialized in a local {@link KeyValueStore} with an internal\\n290:      * store name. Note that store name may not be queryable through Interactive Queries.\\n291:      * An internal changelog topic is created by default. Note that store name may not be queryable through Interactive Queries.\\n313:      * An internal changelog topic is created by default. Because the source topic can\\n314:      * be used for recovery, you can avoid creating the changelog topic by setting\\n315:      * the {@code \\\"topology.optimization\\\"} to {@code \\\"all\\\"} in the {@link StreamsConfig}.\\n316:      *\\n317:      * @param topic     the topic name; cannot be {@code null}\\n318:      * @param consumed  the instance of {@link Consumed} used to define optional parameters; cannot be {@code null}\\n319:      * @return a {@link KTable} for the specified topic\\n320:      */\\n321:     public synchronized <K, V> KTable<K, V> table(final String topic,\\n322:                                                   final Consumed<K, V> consumed) {\\n323:         Objects.requireNonNull(topic, \\\"topic can't be null\\\");\\n324:         Objects.requireNonNull(consumed, \\\"consumed can't be null\\\");\\n325:         final ConsumedInternal<K, V> consumedInternal = new ConsumedInternal<>(consumed);\\n326: \\n327:         final MaterializedInternal<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materializedInternal =\\n328:             new MaterializedInternal<>(\\n329:                 Materialized.with(consumedInternal.keySerde(), consumedInternal.valueSerde()),\\n330:                 internalStreamsBuilder,\\n331:                 topic + \\\"-\\\");\\n332: \\n333:         return internalStreamsBuilder.table(topic, consumedInternal, materializedInternal);\\n334:     }\\n335: \\n336:     /**\\n337:      * Create a {@link KTable} for the specified topic.\\n338:      * The default {@code \\\"auto.offset.reset\\\"} strategy as specified in the {@link StreamsConfig config} are used.\\n339:      * Key and value deserializers as defined by the options in {@link Materialized} are used.\\n340:      * Input {@link KeyValue records} with {@code null} key will be dropped.\\n341:      * <p>\\n342:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\\n343:      * If this is not the case the returned {@link KTable} will be corrupted.\\n344:      * <p>\\n345:      * The resulting {@link KTable} will be materialized in a local {@link KeyValueStore} using the {@link Materialized} instance.\\n346:      * An internal changelog topic is created by default. This also means that the work\\n188:      * will not be parallelized for multiple topics, and the number of tasks will scale with the maximum partition\\n189:      * count of any matching topic rather than the total number of partitions across all topics.\\n190:      * <p>\\n191:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\\n192:      * If this is not the case it is the user's responsibility to repartition the data before any key based operation\\n193:      * (like aggregation or join) is applied to the returned {@link KStream}.\\n194:      *\\n195:      * @param topicPattern the pattern to match for topic names\\n196:      * @return a {@link KStream} for topics matching the regex pattern.\\n197:      */\\n198:     public synchronized <K, V> KStream<K, V> stream(final Pattern topicPattern) {\\n199:         return stream(topicPattern, Consumed.with(null, null));\\n200:     }\\n201: \\n202:     /**\\n203:      * Create a {@link KStream} from the specified topic pattern.\\n204:      * The {@code \\\"auto.offset.reset\\\"} strategy, {@link TimestampExtractor}, key and value deserializers\\n205:      * are defined by the options in {@link Consumed} are used.\\n206:      * <p>\\n207:      * If multiple topics are matched by the specified pattern, the created {@link KStream} will read data from all of\\n208:      * them and there is no ordering guarantee between records from different topics. This also means that the work\\n209:      * will not be parallelized for multiple topics, and the number of tasks will scale with the maximum partition\\n210:      * count of any matching topic rather cannot be {@code null}\\n263:      * @return a {@link KTable} for the specified topic\\n264:      */\\n265:     public synchronized <K, V> KTable<K, V> table(final String topic,\\n266:                                                   final Consumed<K, V> consumed,\\n267:                                                   final Materialized<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materialized) {\\n268:         Objects.requireNonNull(topic, \\\"topic can't be null\\\");\\n269:         Objects.requireNonNull(consumed, \\\"consumed can't be null\\\");\\n270:         Objects.requireNonNull(materialized, \\\"materialized can't be null\\\");\\n271:         final ConsumedInternal<K, V> consumedInternal = new ConsumedInternal<>(consumed);\\n272:         materialized.withKeySerde(consumedInternal.keySerde()).withValueSerde(consumedInternal.valueSerde());\\n273: \\n274:         final MaterializedInternal<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materializedInternal =\\n275:             new MaterializedInternal<>(materialized, internalStreamsBuilder, topic + \\\"-\\\");\\n276: \\n277:         return internalStreamsBuilder.table(topic, consumedInternal, materializedInternal);\\n278:     }\\n279: \\n280:     /**\\n281:      * Create a {@link KTable} for the specified topic.\\n282:      * The default {@code \\\"auto.offset.reset\\\"} strategy and default key and value deserializers as specified in the\\n283:      * {@link StreamsConfig config} are used.\\n284:      * Input {@link KeyValue records} with {@code null} key will be dropped.\\n285:      * <p>\\n286:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\\n287:      * If this is not the case the returned {@link KTable} will be corrupted.\\n288:      * <p>\\n289:      * The resulting {@link KTable} will be materialized in a local {@link KeyValueStore} with an internal\\n290:      * store name. \\n516: \\n517:     /**\\n518:      * Adds a state store to the underlying {@link Topology}.\\n519:      * <p>\\n520:      * It is required to connect state stores to {@link Creating a single {@link Processor} object\\n545:      * and returning the same object reference in {@link ProcessorSupplier#get()} is a\\n546:      * violation of the supplier pattern and leads to runtime exceptions.\\n547:      * This {@link Processor} should be used to keep the {@link StateStore} up-to-date.\\n548:      * The default {@link TimestampExtractor} as specified in the {@link StreamsConfig config} is used.\\n549:      * <p>\\n550:      * It is not required to connect a global store to the {@link Processor Processors},\\n551:      * or {@link org.apache.kafka.streams.kstream.KTable#transformValues(ValueTransformerWithKeySupplier, String...) ValueTransformer};\\n552:      * those have read-only access to all global stores by default.\\n553:      *\\n554:      * @param storeBuilder          user defined {@link StoreBuilder}; can't be import java.util.regex.Pattern;\n48: \n49: /**\n50:  * {@code StreamsBuilder} provides the high-level Kafka Streams DSL to specify a Kafka Streams topology.\n51:  *\n52:  * <p>\n53:  * It is a requirement that the processing logic ({@link Topology}) be defined in a deterministic way,\n54:  * as in, the order in which all operators are added must be predictable and the same across all application\n55:  * instances.\n56:  * Topologies are only identical if all operators are added in the same order.\n57:  * If different {@link KafkaStreams} instances of the same application build different topologies the result may be\n58:  * incompatible runtime code and unexpected results or errors\n59:  *\n60:  * @see Topology\n61:  * @see KStream\n62:  * @see KTable\n63:  * @see This also means that the work\n188:      * will not be parallelized for multiple topics, and the number of tasks will scale with the maximum partition\n189:      * count of any matching topic rather than the total number of partitions across all topics.\n190:      * <p>\n191:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\n192:      * If this is not the case it is the user's responsibility to repartition the data before any key based operation\n193:      * (like aggregation or join) is applied to the returned {@link KStream}.\n194:      *\n195:      * @param topicPattern the pattern to match for topic names\n196:      * @return a {@link KStream} for topics matching the regex pattern.\n197:      */\n198:     public synchronized <K, V> KStream<K, V> stream(final Pattern topicPattern) {\n199:         return stream(topicPattern, Consumed.with(null, null));\n200:     }\n201: \n202:     /**\n203:      * Create a {@link KStream} from the specified topic pattern.\n204:      * The {@code \"auto.offset.reset\"} strategy, {@link TimestampExtractor}, key and value deserializers\n205:      * are defined by the options in {@link Consumed} are used.\n206:      * <p>\n207:      * If multiple topics are matched by the specified pattern, the created {@link KStream} will read data from all of\n208:      * them and there is no ordering guarantee between records from different topics. This also means that the work\n209:      * will not be parallelized for multiple topics, and the number of tasks will scale with the maximum partition\n210:      * count of any matching topic rather topics matching the regex pattern.\n219:      */\n220:     public synchronized <K, V> KStream<K, V> stream(final Pattern topicPattern,\n221:                                                     final {@code \"auto.offset.reset\"} strategy, {@link TimestampExtractor}, key and value deserializers\n230:      * are defined by the options in {@link Consumed} are used.\n231:      * Input {@link KeyValue records} with {@code null} key will be dropped.\n232:      * <p>\n233:      * Note that the specified input topic must be partitioned by key.\n234:      * If this is not the case the returned {@link instance.\n238:      * An internal changelog topic is created by default. Because the source topic can\n239:      * be used for recovery, you can avoid creating the changelog topic by setting\n240:      * the {@code \"topology.optimization\"} to {@code \"all\"} in the {@link StreamsConfig}.\n241:      * <p>\n242:      * You should only specify serdes in the {@link Consumed} instance as these will also be used to overwrite the\n243:      * serdes in {@link Materialized}, i.e.,\n244:      * <pre> {@code\n245:      * streamBuilder.table(topic, Consumed.with(Serde.String(), Serde.String()), Materialized.<String, String, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>as(storeName))\n246:      * }\n247:      * </pre>\n248:      * To query the local {@link ReadOnlyKeyValueStore} it must be obtained via\n249:      * {@link KafkaStreams#store(StoreQueryParameters) KafkaStreams#store(...)}:\n250:      * <pre>{@code\n251:      * KafkaStreams streams = ...\n252:      * StoreQueryParameters<ReadOnlyKeyValueStore<K, ValueAndTimestamp<V>>> storeQueryParams = StoreQueryParameters.fromNameAndType(queryableStoreName, QueryableStoreTypes.timestampedKeyValueStore());\n253:      * ReadOnlyKeyValueStore<K, ValueAndTimestamp<V>> localStore = streams.store(storeQueryParams);\n254:      * K key = \"some-key\";\n255:      * ValueAndTimestamp<V> valueForKey = localStore.get(key); // key must be local (application state is shared over all running Kafka Streams instances)\n256:      * }</pre>\n257:      * For non-local keys, a custom RPC mechanism must be implemented using {@link KafkaStreams#metadataForAllStreamsClients()} to\n258:      * query the value of the key on a parallel running instance of your Kafka Streams application.\n259:      *\n260:      * @param topic              the topic name; cannot be {@code null}\n261:      * @param consumed           the instance of {@link Consumed} used to define optional parameters; cannot be {@code null}\n262:      * @param materialized       the instance of {@link Materialized} used to materialize a state store; cannot be {@code null}\n263:      * @return a {@link KTable} for the specified topic\n264:      */\n265:     public synchronized <K, V> KTable<K, V> table(final String topic,\n266:                                                   final Consumed<K, V> consumed,\n267:                                                   final Materialized<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materialized) {\n268:         Objects.requireNonNull(topic, \"topic can't be null\");\n269:         Objects.requireNonNull(consumed, \"consumed can't be null\");\n270:         Objects.requireNonNull(materialized, \"materialized can't be null\");\n271:         final ConsumedInternal<K, V> consumedInternal = new ConsumedInternal<>(consumed);\n272:         materialized.withKeySerde(consumedInternal.keySerde()).withValueSerde(consumedInternal.valueSerde());\n273: \n274:         final MaterializedInternal<K, V, KeyValueStore<Bytes, byte[]>> materializedInternal =\n275:             new MaterializedInternal<>(materialized, internalStreamsBuilder, topic + \"-\");\n276: \n277:         return internalStreamsBuilder.table(topic, consumedInternal, materializedInternal);\n278:     }\n279: \n280:     /**\n281:      * Create a {@link KTable} for the specified topic.\n282:      * The default {@code \"auto.offset.reset\"} strategy and default key and value deserializers as specified in the\n283:      * {@link StreamsConfig config} are used.\n284:      * Input {@link KeyValue records} with {@code null} key will be dropped.\n285:      * <p>\n286:      * Note that the specified input topics must be partitioned by key.\n287:      * If this is not the case the returned {@link KTable} will be corrupted.\n288:      * <p>\n289:      * The resulting {@link KTable} will be materialized in a local {@link KeyValueStore} with an internal\n290:      * store name. Note that store name may not be queryable through Interactive Queries.\n374:      * No internal changelog topic is created since the original input topic can be used for recovery (cf.\n375:      * methods of {@link KGroupedStream} and {@link KGroupedTable} that return a {@link KTable}).\n376:      * <p>\n377:      * Note that {@link GlobalKTable} always applies {@code \"auto.offset.reset\"} strategy {@code \"earliest\"}\n378:      * regardless of the specified value in {@link StreamsConfig} or {@link Consumed}.\n379:      * Furthermore, {@link GlobalKTable} cannot be a {@link org.apache.kafka.streams.state.VersionedBytesStoreSupplier\n380:      * versioned state store}.\n381:      *\n382:      * @param topic the topic name; Note that store name may not be queryable through Interactive Queries.\n409:      * No internal changelog topic is created since the original input topic can be used for recovery (cf.\n410:      * methods of {@link KGroupedStream} and {@link KGroupedTable} that return a {@link KTable}).\n411:      * <p>\n412:      * Note that {@link GlobalKTable} always applies {@code \"auto.offset.reset\"} strategy {@code \"earliest\"}\n413:      * regardless of the specified value in {@link StreamsConfig}.\n414:      * Furthermore, {@link GlobalKTable} cannot be a {@link Consumed.with(null, null));\n422:     }\n423: \n424:     /**\n425:      * Create a {@link GlobalKTable} for the specified topic.\n426:      * <p>\n427:      * Input {@link KeyValue} pairs with {@code {@link Materialized}.\n431:      * However, no internal changelog topic is created since the original input topic can be used for recovery (cf.\n432:      * methods of {@link KGroupedStream} and
